     "[| Equiv_Exec ?m ?equiv_states12.0 ?localState1.0 ?localState2.0
          ?input_fun1.0 ?input_fun2.0 ?output_fun1.0 ?output_fun2.0
          ?trans_fun1.0 ?trans_fun2.0 ?k1.0 ?k2.0 ?c1.0 ?c2.0;

          ?input_fun2.0 ?input_fun3.0 ?output_fun2.0 ?output_fun3.0
          ?trans_fun2.0 ?trans_fun3.0 ?k2.0 ?k3.0 ?c2.0 ?c3.0;
         ?equiv_states13.0 =
         (%s1 s3.
             (if s1 = ?localState1.0 ?c1.0 & s3 = ?localState3.0 ?c3.0
